I need to analyze the Ground Truth (GT) and compare each candidate to it.

## Ground Truth Analysis

The GT is:
$$f(\epsilon, T) = 55.83\epsilon(-0.0970(T - 325.31) + 1) + 6.648\epsilon \exp(-(T - 325.31)^2)$$

Expanding the first term:
$$= 55.83\epsilon \cdot (-0.0970T + 0.0970 \times 325.31 + 1) + 6.648\epsilon \exp(-(T-325.31)^2)$$
$$= -5.414\epsilon T + 55.83\epsilon(1 + 31.54) + 6.648\epsilon \exp(-(T-325.31)^2)$$

Wait, let me be more careful:
$$= 55.83\epsilon(-0.0970T + 0.0970 \times 325.31 + 1) + 6.648\epsilon \exp(-(T-325.31)^2)$$
$$= -5.414\epsilon T + 55.83\epsilon(31.54 + 1) + 6.648\epsilon \exp(-(T-325.31)^2)$$

So the GT has the structure:
$$f = a \cdot \epsilon \cdot T + b \cdot \epsilon + c \cdot \epsilon \cdot \exp(-(T - d)^2)$$

Key basis functions in GT:
1. $\epsilon \cdot T$ (linear in both)
2. $\epsilon$ (linear)
3. $\epsilon \cdot \exp(-(T-d)^2)$ (Gaussian in T, linear in epsilon)

The Gaussian $\exp(-(T-d)^2)$ is critical. This can be written as $\exp(-T^2 + 2dT - d^2) = e^{-d^2}\exp(-T^2 + 2dT)$.

Now let me check each candidate for the presence of these basis functions.

### Key observations for filtering:

The GT is **linear in epsilon** (every term has exactly one factor of epsilon). The GT has a **Gaussian dependence on T** via $\exp(-(T-c)^2)$.

Let me check candidates systematically:

**Candidates without T-dependence at all (only epsilon):** 5, 15, 19, 22, 23, 34, 42, 45, 48, 49 — These cannot match since GT depends on T. **[NO MATCH]** for all of these.

**Candidates with wrong T-dependence structure:**

For the Gaussian $\exp(-(T-c)^2)$, I need something that can produce this. Let me look for $\exp(T \cdot c)$ terms (which give exponential, not Gaussian), $\log(T)$ terms, $\sin/\cos(T)$ terms, etc.

The Gaussian $\exp(-(T-c)^2) = \exp(-c^2)\exp(2cT)\exp(-T^2)$. A single exponential $\exp(aT)$ cannot produce $\exp(-T^2)$. So candidates with only $\exp(cT)$ type T-dependence cannot match.
